[[Reload the page->Network tab 2 (reload)]] [[Go back->Start]]When you reload the page, everything loads instantly. It looks like whatever was happening slowly last time was cached this time. <<newinfo "Something is being cached">> [[Go back->Start]]You reload the page. It reloads instantly. A bunch of information appears in the network tab, but you realize it's going to be a waste of time to even look at it -- you aren't going to be able to figure out what's slow. [[Try a different website ->Network tab 3 neopets]]You keep the network tab open, and type "neopets.com" into the address bar. You haven't been to that site in years. You sit there waiting for 60 seconds. It's extremely slow to load, just like google.com was. It looks like the "DNS Resolution" step took 5 seconds. <<newinfo "Some DNS requests are taking 5 seconds">> [[Think about why DNS might be slow->DNS diagnosis]]Now we know that some DNS queries are slow. Why might that be? [[Use dig to make some DNS queries from the command line->Dig 1]] [[Find out which DNS server your browser is using->Tcpdump]]You run <code>dig neopets.com</code>. Here's the output you see: <pre> $ dig neopets.com ; <<>> DiG 9.16.13 <<>> neopets.com ;; global options: +cmd ;; Got answer: ;; ->>HEADER<<- opcode: QUERY, status: NOERROR, id: 1624 ;; flags: qr rd ra; QUERY: 1, ANSWER: 1, AUTHORITY: 0, ADDITIONAL: 1 ;; OPT PSEUDOSECTION: ; EDNS: version: 0, flags:; udp: 4096 ; COOKIE: 9a8217ed002ab529010000006076f4b55f1e8fcfca9af2e7 (good) ;; QUESTION SECTION: ;neopets.com. IN A ;; ANSWER SECTION: neopets.com. 3600 IN A 23.96.35.235 ;; Query time: 23 msec ;; SERVER: 8.8.8.8#53(8.8.8.8) ;; WHEN: Wed Apr 14 09:57:46 EDT 2021 ;; MSG SIZE rcvd: 84 </pre> That's weird, you think -- it says <code>Query time: 23 msec</code> in the output, but you know your other DNS query was taking 5 seconds. [[Go back->DNS diagnosis]]You want to figure out what DNS server your browser is using, so you decide to use tcpdump. You know that DNS servers usually use port 53, so you just look for traffic on port 53. <pre> $ sudo tcpdump -n -i any port 53 tcpdump: data link type LINUX_SLL2 tcpdump: verbose output suppressed, use -v[v]... for full protocol decode listening on any, link-type LINUX_SLL2 (Linux cooked v2), snapshot length 262144 bytes </pre> [[Wait for a couple of minutes->Tcpdump wait]] [[Load a webpage in your browser->Tcpdump browser]]You wait for a while, but no output appears. Looks like there aren't any DNS queries. That's weird...You leave <code>tcpdump</code> open, and open your browser. You've been thinking of buying a guitar, so you open the guitar seller's website. It starts loading really slowly [[Switch back to the tcpdump terminal window->Tcpdump output 2]]When you go back to your terminal after loading the website in your browser, there's suddenly a lot of output there. It looks like this: <pre> wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.55742: 11198 3/0/0 CNAME c-ca00.kvcdn.com., CNAME p-camo00.kxcdn.com., A 51.222.8.159 (122) wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.55742: 41144 3/0/0 CNAME c-ca00.kvcdn.com., CNAME p-camo00.kxcdn.com., AAAA 2607:5300:203:769f::1 (134) wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.36042: 47068 4/0/0 A 151.101.66.133, A 151.101.130.133, A 151.101.194.133, A 151.101.2.133 (97) wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.36042: 3269 0/0/0 (33) wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.32872: 26122 1/0/0 A 34.117.61.88 (48) wlp3s0 In IP 192.168.1.1.53 > 192.168.1.121.32872: 37891 0/1/0 (128) wlp3s0 Out IP 192.168.1.121.56455 > 192.168.1.1.53: 26777+ A? api.appmate.io. What is it? What's the IP address of the DNS server? <<textbox "$dns_server_guess" "" "Tcpdump DNS server">> [[I don't know->Tcpdump DNS server]]<<if $dns_server_guess eq "192.168.1.1">> That's right! It's 192.168.1.1 <<else>> The DNS server's IP address is <strong>192.168.1.1</strong>. <<if def $dns_server_guess>> You guessed <<print $dns_server_guess>>. <</if>> <</if>> We can see that by looking at this line (or any line) in the tcpdump output: <code>wlp3s0 Out IP 192.168.1.121.38308 > <strong>192.168.1.1.53</strong>: 49281+ AAAA? fonts.gstatic.com. (35)</code>
